3b5('dul ba): shes ldan dag kho bo cag lus drud nas khrus byas pa yino//'phags pa dag ci dge sbyong khyed 'dod pa'i yon tan gyis gzir tam/bkren pa khyed kyi mgrin pa rdog pas

4a7('dul ba): ldan 'das la rgyas par gsol to//bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/dge slong dag de ltar na snga ma ni bcas la'o//'di ni gnang ba yin te/de lta bas na dge slong
4b1('dul ba): gis rkang pa so phag gis drud par gnang //lus gzhan ni ma yin te/'drud na 'gal tshabs can du 'gyur ro//bcom ldan 'das yangs pa can na spre'u rdzing gi 'gram khang pa brtsegs pa na

4b6('dul ba): smras pa/'di la ci zhig 'tshal bar bgyi/bram ze rgan pa rgan pa rnams ni gus par smra bar bya ba yin la/dge slong rnams ni phyag bya ba yin na/de ci'i phyir khyed dge slong rnams

7a1('dul ba): bram ze dang khyim bdag 'ongs shing lhags pa rnams la chos bstan par mi bya/bram ze dang /khyim bdag gi khyi ma rnam su 'gro bar mi bya'i//nam sos par gyur pa
7a2('dul ba): de'i tshe khrus byas nas dri ma med par gyur pa dang /dge 'dun gyi nang du 'dug par bya/bram ze dang khyim bdag 'ongs shing lhags pa rnams la chos bstan par bya//bram ze dang khyi ba dag

7a4('dul ba): ze dang khyim bdag dad pa tsA dag dge slong rnams la dri 'bul ba na/dge slong rnams 'gyod nas mi len pa dang /de dag gis smras pa/'phags pa dag gang gi tshe sangs rgyas bcom

7b1('dul ba): stsal pa/blang bar bya'o//dge slong rnams kyis blangs nas de dag nyid kyi mdun du bor ba dang /de dag gis smras pa/'phags pa dag bdag cag gis/rin thang bzhin du nyo nyon khyed

8a5('dul ba): kyis smras pa/'phags pa rgyal bu rtogs byed kyis khang bzangs pad+ma ris tshon brgya rtsa gcig gis bkra bar byas pa/khyed kyis gzhig gam ci/nyi dga' bos smras pa/
8a6('dul ba): bkren pa rtogs byed 'di la lhag par chags pas dus byas nas gar skye gtol medo//khyed kyang 'di la lhags par chags pas dus byas nas yi dgas lba ba can rna mas kyi nang
8a7('dul ba): du skye bar 'gyuraro//de dag kha zer ba'i skabs de/dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyi dgongs pa/nyes dmigs gang cung

8b2('dul ba): bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong gis ka ba li lag pas bsnun par mi byaM zhes bka' stsal pa dang /drug sde rnams khu tshur dang /gru mo dang /phrag pa dang /mgo dang /rtsib logs
8b3('dul ba): dang /rgya ba dang /rked pa dang /brla dang /pus mo dang /byin pa dang /rkang pa dang /dbyug pa dang /bong ba dang /gzhan gyis bsnun par byed pa nyes dmigs de nyid du gyur
8b4('dul ba): nas/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/gang gis kyang bsnun par mi bya'o//drug sde rnams rtsig pa dang /sa dang gzhan la basbyin par byed pa dang /bcom ldan 'das
8b5('dul ba): kyis bka' stsal pa/gzhan la yang gang dag gis bsnun par mi bya'o//snun na 'gal chibs can du 'gyuraro//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyu le bu rgyal
8b6('dul ba): byed kyi tshul mgon myed zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhig so//drug sde rnams snga dro mnyan yod du bsod snyoms kyi phyir zhugs pa dang /de rnams kyis bram ze zhig tshangs pa
8b7('dul ba): skud pa thogs te/slongs mo la rgyu zhing /des bza' ba dang bca' bo yang ming du skyed pa mthong nas/drug sde rnams kyis smras pa/dga' bo nye dga' bo//thabs 'di ni bzang
9a1('dul ba): po zhig ste bdag cag kyang de lta bu bya'o zhes de dag phyi de nyin tshangs pa'i skud pa thogs te/bsod snyos la zhugs pa ma dad pa rnams kyis mthong nas/'phya zhing gus par smra'o/

9a3('dul ba): gis smras pa/'di la ci zhig 'tshal bar bgyi/bram ze rgan pa rgan pa rnams ni gus par smra bar bya ba yin la/dge slong rnams ni phyag bya ba yin na/de ci'i phyir khyed dge slong rnams la
9a4('dul ba): gus par smra bar byed kyis phyag ma yin/'phags pa dag bdag cag gis khyed bram ze lags par 'tshal gyi dge slong du ni ma lag so//de lta lags pas bdag cag gis ma 'tshal gyis
9a5('dul ba): bzod par gsol zhes byas pa dang /de dag cang mi smra bar 'dug/skabs de dge slong rnams kyi thos nas bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa//nyes
9a6('dul ba): dmigs gang cung zad ci 'byung ba ni dge slong rnams tshangs pa'i skud pa thogs pa las gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong gis tshangs pa'i skud pa gdags par mi bya'o//'dogs na 'gal
9a7('dul ba): tshabs can du 'gyuraro//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhug so//drug sde rnams snga dro sha
9b1('dul ba): thabs dang chos gos bgos lhung bzed thogs te/mnyan yod du bsod snyoms kyi phyir zhugs pa na/de dag gis bram ze dri dang me tog gis brgyan pa tshon sna lnga pa'i skud pas lag pa bcings
9b2('dul ba): pa zhig dus ston zos nas dbang po tshim ste/khyim nas byung ba mthong ba dang /de dag gis smras pa/dga' bo nyi dga' bo thabs 'di ni bzangs po zhig ste/bdag cag kyang 'di bzhin bya'o/
9b3('dul ba): zhes/de dag byi de nyin tshon sna lnga pa'i skud pas lag pa bcings nas/bsod snyoms la zhugs pa/bram ze dang khyim bdag rnams kyis mthong nas/'phya zhing gus par smra'o gus par spro'o
9b4('dul ba): zhes smras pa dang /drug sde rnams kyis smras pa/bkren pa khyed kyis gus par smra bar bya ba gang dag yin pa dang /phyag bya ba gang dag yin pa 'di yang mi shes sam/de dag gis smras
9b5('dul ba): ba/'di la ci zhig 'tshale bar bgyi/bram ze rgan pa rgan pa rnams ni/gus par smra bar bya ba yin la/dge slong rnams ni phyag bya ba yin na/de ci'i phyir/khyed dge slong rnams
9b6('dul ba): la gus par smra bar byed kyi phyag ma yin/'phags pa dag bdag cag gis khyed bram ze lags par 'tshal gyi/dge slong du ni mo lag so//de lta lags pas bdag cag gis ma
9b7('dul ba): 'tshal gyis bzod par gsol lo zhes byas pa dang /de dag cang mi smra bar 'dug/skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan
10a1('dul ba): 'das kyi dgongs pa/nyes dmigs gang cung zad ci byung ba ni dge slong rnams tshon sna lnga pa'i skud pas lag pa 'ching ba las gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong
10a2('dul ba): gis tshon sna lnga pa'i skud pas lag pa bcing bar mi bya'o//'chang na 'grol tshabs can du 'gyur ro//bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong tshon sna lnga pa'i skud pas lag pa bcing
10a3('dul ba): bar mi bya'o zhes bka' stsal pa dang /dge slong nad pa gzhan zhig sman pa'i drung du song ste/bzhin bzangs kho bo le nad 'di lta bu byung na sman ston cig ces byas pa dang /des
10a4('dul ba): smras pa/'phags pa skud pa la gsang sngags dag gis bzlas brjod byas te/lag pa la bcings na khyod 'tsho bar 'gyur ro//des smras pa/bzhin bzangs bcom ldan 'das
10a5('dul ba): kyis ma gnang ngo //'phags pa khyod kyi ston pa ni thugs rje can yin pas/gnang bar 'gyuraro//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /
10a6('dul ba): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de lta bas na gnang gis//sman pa'i lung gis skud pa bcang bar bya'o//bcom ldan 'das kyis sman pa'i lung gis skud pa tsam
10a7('dul ba): par bya'o//zhes bka' stsal pa dang /dge slong rnams lags pa g.yes pa'i rtse mo la'i tsheng ste/nyes dmigs de nyid du gyur nas/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
10b1('dul ba): 28dge slong dag lag pa g.yas pa'i rtse mo las cung bar mi bya'o de rnams lag pa g.yas pa'i dpung pa la 'ching ste/nyes dmigs de nyid gyur nas/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
10b2('dul ba): stsal pa/lag pa g.yas pa'i dpung pa la bcing bar mi bya'o//de rnams lag pa g.yon pa'i rtse myo la 'ching ste/nyes dmigs de nyi du gyur nas/bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal
10b3('dul ba): pa/lag pa g.yon pa'i rtse mo la bcing bar mi bya'i/'on kyang lag pa g.yon pa'i dpung pa la bcing bar bya'o//dge slong rnams nad sos par gyur nas/skud pa bab bab tu 'dor
10b4('dul ba): ba mi ma yin pa rnams 'phya ste/'phags pa dag nged kyis sos par byas nas/da ma gus par byed pa lta/skabs de dge slong rnams kyis/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom
10b5('dul ba): ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/bab bab tu dor bar mi bya ste/gal te nad ma byang na chos gos kyi mtha' 'am/rgya cang la bcing bar bya'o//'on te thams cad kyi thams cad sos
10b6('dul ba): pipar gyur nas//ka ba'i saur ka 'am/rtsig pa'i gseb tu gzhugs par bya'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun
10b7('dul ba): dga'i ra ba na bzhud so//drug sde rnams snga dro sham thabs dang chos gos bgos/lhung bzed thogs te mnyan yod du bsod snyoms kyi phyir zhugs pa na/bram ze dang /khyim
11a1('dul ba): bdag rnams kyi rgyan slo ma'i nang du gzhag pa drug sde rnams kyis rkang rgyan dang lag rgyun dgra thogs nas/smras pa/dga' bo nye dga' bo ji ltar mdzes sam/
11a2('dul ba): bram ze dang /khyim bdag gis smras pa/'phags pa khyed mgo ni phyi/mchen khung ni spun 'di la lus mdzes pa ci zhig yod//gdon mi za bar dge sbyong khyed 'dod pa'i yon tan dag gi
11a3('dul ba): gzer bar gyur to zhes byas pa dang /de rnams cad mi smra bar 'dug/skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis
11a4('dul ba): dgongs pa/nyes dmigs gang cung zad ci byung ba ni/dge slong rnams lag rgyan dang rkang rgyan dag gis bdag nyid brgyan pa las gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong gis lag
11a5('dul ba): rgyan dang rkang rgyan gyis bdag nyid brgyan par mi bya'o//brgyan na 'gal tshabs can du 'gyur ro//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na/rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi
11a6('dul ba): tshotshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba ni bzhugaso//gtsug lag khang du mi byin par len pa rnams kyis/dge 'dun gyi mdzod dang gang zag gis gnas khang dag
11a7('dul ba): nas brkus//dge slong gzhan dag cig yang stor ni/bdag cag gi stor nas ji tsam lon pa mtsho ro//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa
11b1('dul ba): dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de lta bas na gnang gis rgya bcang bar bya'o//bcom ldan 'das kyis rgya bcang bar bya'o zhes bka' stsal pa dang /drug sde rnams kyis
11b2('dul ba): gser dang /dngul dang /bai DUr+ya dang /shel las byas pa dang /sor gdub rgyu rgyun sna tshogs kyi sku be rgyan pa dag bcang so//de nas bram ze dang khyim bdag dag mthong nas/lag
11b3('dul ba): pab brkyang ste smras pa/bzhin bzings nad med cig nad mod cig/de dag gis smras pa/'phags pa 'di ci lags/bzhin bzangs bcom ldan 'das kyis rgya gnang //de dag 'phya
11b4('dul ba): smod kha zer zhing /dge sbyong shAkya'i bu rnams kyi dge sbyong gi tshul nyams shing tshangs pa'i tshul nyams te/'di ni da ltar rgya la tha snyad 'dogs shing /rgyan rnams kyis bdag nyid
11b5('dul ba): brgyan par byed do//skangs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/dge slong gos gser dang /dngul dang /
11b6('dul ba): bai DUr+ya dang /shel las byas pa'i rgyu ba cang bar mi bya/sor gdub rgya yang bcang bar mi bya'i/'on kyang rgyu lnga por gan dang /zangs las byas pa dang /khur ba las byas pa dang
11b7('dul ba): ba so las byas pa dang /ro las byas pa bcang bar bya'o//drug sngo rnams kyis rgyal skyes pa dang /bud med nyal po byed pa bris pa dang /bram ze dang /khyim bdag rnams kyis
12a1('dul ba): smras pa/'phags pa ci dge sbyong khyed 'dod pa'i yon tan dag gis gzir tam/gnas skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /
12a2('dul ba): ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/rgyu ni gnyis te dge 'dun gyis dang /gang zag gi'o//de la dge 'dun gyi ni dbus 'khor mo bris la/blo gnyis ri dgas/'og tu gtsug
12a3('dul ba): leg khang gi bdag po'i ming bri bar bya'o//gang zag ni rus pa'i keng rus sam/mgo'i thod pa bri bar bya'o//sdom ni/sen mo 'dreg dang byi dor dang //a mra dang ni skyu ru ra//lhung ban
12a4('dul ba): brgyad po bkag pa dang /rje su gnang ba gnyis yino//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshil mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba ni bzhug so//gang gi
12a5('dul ba): tshe khyim bdag mgon med rjes sbyin gyi sangs rgyas la sogs pa/dge slong gi dge 'dun lo//rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal phul ba de'i tshe/des 'dreg mkhan gyi me la smras pa/
12a6('dul ba): skyes bu rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal du song la/'phags pa rnams kyi sgra dang kha spu regs shig/de rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal du song ba dang /drug sde rnams kyi kun tu spyod pa ni/
12a7('dul ba): drug sde gong yang rung po zhig gis//rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshol gyi sgo mi stongs pa yin te/tshe dang ldan pa nye dga' bo rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal na 'chag cing 'dug pa des de rkyang
12b1('dul ba): ring po nas mthong nas smras pa/bzhin bzangs 'ongs pa legaso//'ongs pa lagaso//khyod zla ba lta bur gnas na ring mo zhig lon te/gang nas 'ongs/des smras pa/'phyags pa khyim
12b2('dul ba): bdag gis 'phags pa rnams kyi sgra dang kha spu bregs pa'i slad du 'dir bta ngo //des smras pa/sen mo legs par 'breg shes sam/'phags pa 'di nyid bdag gi bzo lag so//
12b3('dul ba): bltas tshur/de nyid nye bar 'ongs pa dang /nyi dga' bos ldeg pa brkyang //'dug mkhan gyis smras pa/'phags pa ci 'dra bar breg/bzhin bzang 'bru'i rtse mo ltar rigs shig/des
12b4('dul ba): 'bru'i rtse mo ltar bregs pa dang /des smras pa/da ni ra ba'i cig lta blo dang /spu dro'i so dang /ste'u ka dang /zla ba chos pa ltar gyis shig/des de ji lta ji ltar bsgo ba de lta de lta bur
12b5('dul ba): byas pa dang /nu drug tu smras pa/bkren pa khyod ko cung zad kyang mi shes pa zhig/'di kho na ltar mnyan par gyis la sang shig/ces des de nyi ma nub kyi bar du ma btang //de
12b6('dul ba): nyi ma nub nas khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin gyi drung du song po dang /mgon med zas byin gyis smras pa/kye skyes bu khyod kyis 'phags pa mang po ji snyed cig gi mgo dang khyu
12b7('dul ba): brags/bdag gas 'phags pa rnams kyi sgra dang kha spu ga le bregs/dge slong gzu lums can nye dga' bos bdage bskor nas/sen mo 'bru'i rtse mo dang /ra ba'i cog dang /
13a1('dul ba): spu gri'i so dang /steru ka dang /zla ba tshes pa lta bur gyis shig ces pa'i rnam pa thams cad bdag gis bgyis pa dang /de nas 'di skad ces/bkren pa
13a2('dul ba): khyod ko cung zad kya mi shes pa zhig/'di kho na ltar mnyam par gyis la song shig ces mchi nas/da bzod kho na shor na ci zhig bgyi/khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin le
13a3('dul ba): por gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung ba rnams la nye bar zhi ba med pa lta zhes 'phya ba la zhugaso//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das lo gsol
13a4('dul ba): ba dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa/nyes dmigs gang cung zad ci byung ba ni/dge slong rnams sen mo 'breg pa las gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong gis sen mo
13a5('dul ba): bres par mi bya'o//'breg na 'gal tshabs can du 'gyur ro//bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong gis sen mo byeg par mi bya'o zhes bka' stsal pa dang /dge slong rnams sen
13a6('dul ba): mo ring po ring por 'dug pa/bram ze dang khyim bdag dag gis mthong nas skyes pa/'phags pa dag ci ste sen mo ring po ring por 'jug/bzhin bzangs bcom ldan 'das kyis
13a7('dul ba): ma gnang ngo //'phags pa ci khyed sen mo bcangs pas dag par 'gyur ram/skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /brjo kyi ga
13b1('dul ba): sbyol ldam ni bcas pa'o//'di ni gnang ba yin te/de lta bas na gnang gis/sgren mo rnams pa gnyis po spu gri'i so dang /ste'u ka lta bur breg par bya'o//bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na//
13b2('dul ba): rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sbyin gyi kun dga' ra ba na bzhugaso//gang gi tshe khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin gyis/sangs rgyas la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun
13b3('dul ba): la zhes bya ba thams cad de kho na bzhin no//khyod sen mo 'chos shes sam/'phags pa ji lta bur bgyi/ser po dang dmar po dang /dkar po dang /gser gyi kha dog lta bur
13b4('dul ba): gyis shig ces pa'i rnam pa thams cad bdag gis bgyis pa dang /de nas 'di skad ces bkren pa khyod ko cung zad kyang mi shes pa zhig/'di kho na ltar mnyam par gyis la song shig/
13b5('dul ba): ces mchi nas/da gzod kho na shor na ci zhig bgyi/khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung ba rnams la nye bar zhi ba med pa lta
13b6('dul ba): zhes 'phya ba la zhugaso//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'ongs la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa/nyes dmigs gang cung zad ci byung
13b7('dul ba): ba ni da dge slong rnams sen mo dag byi dor byed pa las gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong gis sen mo dag byi dor mi bya'o//byed na 'gal tshangs can du 'gyur ro//bcom ldan 'das
14a1('dul ba): kyis rwa dge slong gis sen mo dag byi dor mi bya'o zhes bka' stsal ba dang /dge slong tshon rtsi'i las dang /lhung bzed kyi las byed pa rnams kyi sen mo dri ma tshugs
14a2('dul ba): la mdog mi sdug par gyur cing //de rnams sen mo de 'dra ba kho na ro bsod snyoms la 'jug/bram ze dang khyim bdag rnams kyis mthong nas smras pa/'phags pa dag khyed ci'i
14a3('dul ba): phyir sen mo 'di lta bu dri ma chags shing mdog mi sdug/de dag gis bsnyad pa dang /de rnams kyis smras pa/'phags pa ci'i phyir dri ma mau dbye/bcom ldan 'das kyis ma gnang //
14a4('dul ba): 'phags pa khyed ci dwe mi'i 'dam bcangs pas bdag par 'gyur ram/skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
14a5('dul ba): stsal pa/dri ma dbyi ba'i phyir sen mo bzhar bar bya'o//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab na 'od ma'i tshil bya ka lan da ka gnas pa na bzhugaso//rgyal po gzugs
14a6('dul ba): can snying po'i kun tu spyod pa ni dus kyis gsar thog 'bru sar pa'am//'bras bu sar po dang ci yang rung de dag dang por dge 'dun la 'bul lo//de'i 'og tu bdag nyid za'o//
14a7('dul ba): de'i blon po rnams kyiso a mra'i shing thog dag phul ba dang /des snum pa/song la 'angags pa rnams la phul cig/de dag gis bgad pa dang /des smras pa/shes ldan dag
14b1('dul ba): ci la dgod/de dag gis smras pa/g+ha ci khyed nga ni 'phags pa rnams la dang por 'bul snyam dgongs kyi/bdug cag gis ches sngar 'phags pa rnams la phul bar ni ma lags sngam/
14b2('dul ba): des smras pa/gal te de ljin/ngas 'a dgos pa rnams la stong ni kun dga' ra ba nyid phul lo//g+ha legs te/rje su yi ring ngo //des phyogs bzhi'i dge slong gi dge 'dun gyi d+hir
14b3('dul ba): stong gi kun dga' ra ba phul nas der dus ston kyang btsug so//de ji ltar yul ma ga d+hA na gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs dus ston la lta bar 'ongs pa a mra'i shing thog smin pa rnams kyis
14b4('dul ba): tshim par gyur pa de ltar shing thog rgyas par gyur to//de dge 'dun la phulo zhe dge slong rnams kyi sau a mra'i 'bras bu shi mi smin pa nyid du zos so//ji tsam na mtshams kyi rgyal po
14b5('dul ba): zhig la a mra dag dgos par gyur nas/des rgyal po gzugs can snying po la pho nye btang ste/grogs po bdag la a mr-i dag dgos kyis bskur ba'i rigaso zhes byas pa dang /
14b6('dul ba): des pho nya de la smras pa dang /kye skyes bungs stong gyi kun drug rar ba de/bangags pa'i dpe 'dun la phul gyis/song la 'phags pa'i dge 'dun rnams la slongs shig/de'o
14b7('dul ba): ma'i tshal du song ba dang /drug sde rnams kyi kun tu spyod pa ni/rtag tu kun dga' ra ba'i sgo mi stongs par byed pa yin te/tshe dang ldan pa nye dga' bo 'di ma'i tshal gyi sgon 'chag cing
15a1('dul ba): 'dug go/de de'i drung tu song nas phyag 'tshal te des smras pa/rgyal po che ge mo zhig gis A mra'i ched du khyed kyi thad du btad na de'i skad du a mu dag stsal
15a2('dul ba): pa'i rig so//des smras pa/kye skyes bu song la a mra dzi tsam dgos pa de tsami long shog/de song nas a mra'i shing rnams kyis drung du bltas na mi snang ste/de slar log nas smras
15a3('dul ba): pa/'phags pa ma mchis//nyo dga' bos de khrid nas kun dga'i ra bar zhugs te/kun dga'i ra ba thams cad bskor nas smras pa//kye skyes bu shing 'di la 'dzegs shig/
15a4('dul ba): des 'dzegs na ma mthong ba dang /nye dga' bos smras pa/kyai skyes bu shar gyi yal gar song /lho dang nub kyi yal gar song /de thams cad du song nas skyo bar gyur te babs nas
15a5('dul ba): smras pa/'phags pa ci kun dga'i ra ba 'di lo 'di la 'bras bu ma chags sam/bzhin bzangs/ji ltar khro re lo re zhing shing thogs yod pa de ltar 'di 'bras bu chag so//'da'
15a6('dul ba): pi ni rlung dang char pas blugs sam/bzhin bzangs rlung dang char pas ma blags kyis/'on kyang kho bo cag bris a mra'i 'bras bu dag ma smin pa nyid du 'tsho so//de slar log nas
15a7('dul ba): rgyal po gzugs can snying po la gsol pa/lha 'phags pa rnams kyis zhal nas/kho bo cag gis a mra'i 'bras bu dag ma smin pa nyi du'i cho so zhes gsungs ngo //des smras pa/
15b1('dul ba): legs te nga la longs spyad pa nyid dgo so zhes byas pa dang /mi de slar song ngo //ji tsam na dus ston la bab pa'i tshe/yul ma ga d+ha na gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs 'dus nas/de dag gis
15b2('dul ba): smras pa/'phags pa dag ci stong gi kun dga' ra ba 'di lo 'di la 'bras bu ma chags sam/bzhin bzangs dag ji ltar lo ro la re zhing shing thog yod pa de ltar 'di 'bras bu chags
15b3('dul ba): maud kyi 'on kyang kho bo cag gis a mra'i 'bras bu dag ma smin pa nyid 'tsho so//'phags pa dag gang nA yul ma ga d+ha nA gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs thams cad a mra smin pa dag gis
15b4('dul ba): tshim par 'gyur ba de khyod kyis 'bras bu ma smin pa kho nar 'tshos te/gang kho bo cag la gnod pa byas pa ni ma legs pa zhipa byaso//des smras pa/'di rgyal pos yul ma ga d+hA
15b5('dul ba): na gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs la byin pa mi yin gyi/'on kyang dge slong gi dge 'dun la phul te/de lta bas na kho bo cag gis ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin zoso//khyed ci gtogs zhes
15b6('dul ba): byas pa dang /de dag 'phya smod kha zer bar byed do//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa/nyes
15b7('dul ba): dmigs gang cung zad ci byung ba ni/dge slong rnams a mra dag za ba les gyur gyis/de lta bas na dge slong gis a mra dag bza' bar mi bya'o//dge slong a mra dag za na 'gal
16a1('dul ba): tshabs can du 'gyuraro//bcom ldan 'das kyis dge sbyong gis a mU dag bza' bar mi bya'o zhes gsungs pa dang /bram ze dang /khyim bdag dad pa can dag/
16a2('dul ba): dge slong rnams la/shing sa ha ga ra'i shing tog dag 'bul ba na/dge slong rnams kyis smras pa/bcom ldan 'das kyis ma gnang ngo //de dag gis smras pa/'phags pa dag
16a3('dul ba): gang gi tshe/sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten du byung bar ma gyur pa zhes bya ba nas/'jig rten 'di nas 'jig rten pha rol tu 'gro 'am/bzhos shig ces bya ba'i
16a4('dul ba): bAr snga ma bzhin no//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis thos nas/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de lta bas na gnang gis mtshan
16a5('dul ba): nyid grub pa yin no zhes byas nas bza' bar bya ste//'di la 'gyod par mi bya'o//de la mtshan nyid grub pa ni 'di dag yin te/tshig tu tshogs pa rnams so//bram ze dang khyim bdag/
16a6('dul ba): da pa can gzhan dag cig/dge slong rnams oM mu'i shing tog smin pa dag 'bul ba na zhes bya ba nas/de bzhin du 'jig rten 'di nas 'jig rten pha rol tu mchi'am/bzhes shig//
16a7('dul ba): ces bya ba'i bar thams cad snga ma bzhi no//skabs de dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol ba dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/de lta bas na gnang gi
16b1('dul ba): mtshan nyid bye brag phyed do zhes byas te bza' bar bya'o//de la mtshan nyid bye brag byed pa ni 'di dag yin te/sha zhugs pa rnams//sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mnyan yod na rgyal du

31a3('dul ba): par bya/skyon ni bsgrag par bya'o zhes bka' stsal na/ji lhung bzed tsam gyi ched du bdag nyid bstan par bya'amo zhes smras nas dong ngo //ji tsam na tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung stobs bcu
31a4('dul ba): pa de phyogs der 'ongs te/khyim bdag la smras pa/khyim bdag 'di ci yin/des ji lta bu yin pa smras pa dang /tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung stobs bcu pas bsams pa/bdag

31b1('dul ba): pa dang /dge slong dag gis smras pa/gnas brtan khyed lhung bzed tsam gyi ched du khyim+b+ha pa'i mdun du rdzu 'phrul rnam par bstan du rung ngam/de tshe dang ldan pa dag rung yang bla mi rung
31b2('dul ba): yang bla ste/byas zin pas di ci byar yang med do zhes zer de'i skabs de/dge slong rnams kyis/bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa dang /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa//dge slong

31b6('dul ba): de dag ni/ma blangs pa ni blang bar mi bya zhing /blangs pa na sman por du longs spyad pas spyad par bya ba yin no//'di ltar lcags dang /sde'i lhung ba da rmi byin gyis brlab tu rung ba

32b6('dul ba): ste/btsal na/sho gam ma phul ba 'ga' yang med par gyur nas/'dron pa dag nged la khyed cag chom po byed par sems som/ci na/yang dang yang du phyir 'gugs par
32b7('dul ba): byed ces smod par byed//de dag gis 'dron pa de dag tshoms gnyi su byas te bkye ba dang /tshoms gang gi nang na bram ze de med pa dag ni de bzhin dong ngo //tshe mos cig shos 'dong ba
33a1('dul ba): na dril de de bzhin du sgra 'byin par byed nas de dag gis de dag kyang de bzhin du tshoms gnyisu byas shing byas shing bkye ba dang //tha mar bram ze de gcig pu rta

33b1('dul ba): pa na der yang kar sha pa na stong gis nyo ba su yang med nas/des rgyal po'i khab kyi tshong 'dus kyang /tshong 'dus ma yino zhes bsgrag so//de na gzhon nu me skyes glang po che la zhon te rgyal

33b3('dul ba): bos shig/de dag gis dri bos nas mo skyes kyis smras pa/bram ze khyed ci'i phyir tshong 'dus 'di tshe 'dus ma so//zhes sgrogs par byed/des smras pa/khyim bdag ras zung 'di lta bu kor sha

33b5('dul ba): ni spyad zin pa zhig/cig ni ma spyad pa zhig pas/ma spyad pa gang yin pa 'di ni kar sha pa na lnga brgya ri/dang spyod pa 'di ni nyi ma brgya lnga bcu ri'o//bram zes smras pa/ci
33b6('dul ba): 'di de lta bur 'gyur ram/me skyos kyis smras pa/bram ze khyod kyis mngon sum du bstan gyis ltos shig ces des ma spyad pa de steng gi na mkha' la bor ba dang //de bskyengs zhing

323b7('dul ba): kyis bza bo la bden par smra ba dkon par ma thos sam/kho ma ni sgra 'dreg mkhos na 'on kyang bcom ldan 'das kyis ma gnang //des skabs de dge slong ma rnams la bsnyad pa dang /
